 The government has become strict about the problem of disconnection between calls made to and from mobile phones
 ab kol drop kii samasya se nipatane ke liye sarkaar ne dilli or mumbai samet kai sthanon par integrated wais rispance system (IVRS) pranaliyaan shuru kii hai
 Through these, the government will take feedback from customers directly about the quality of the call
 ek aadhikarik vijyapti main bataaya gaya ki sarkaar is par milane vaali pratikriya ko sevapradaataaon ke saath saajha karegi jisase ki vah sudharatmak kadam uthaa saken
 This system will soon be rolled out across the country
 vijyapti ke anusaar, doorsanchaar vibhaag ne is seva ko dilli, mumbai, punjab, uttar pradesh, uttarakhand, maharashtra or goa main 23 disambar se shuru kiya he
 The comments graahakon ko 1955 number se ek iviares kol aayega jis par unhen kuch sawaalon ke jawaab dene honge jinke aadhaar par yah pataa lagaaya jaae ki ki unke kshetra main kol drop kii samasya ke kya haal hai
 If customers want, they can also give their response by smsing toll free to this number
 is par doorsanchaar rajya mantri (swatantra prabhaar) manoj sinha ne kaha ki graahakon se sidhe pratikriya praapt karne ke liye is manch ko shuru kiya gaya he taaki unhen di ja rahi seva kii gunvattta main sudhaar laayaa ja sake
 Initially, only call drop response will be taken from it
 baad main is seva ke madhyam se sampurna doorsanchaar seva ke bare main pratikriyaayein ekatrit kii jaaengi
 An official release said that the government will share the feedback received with service providers so that they can take corrective steps
 is pranali ko jald hi puure desh main shuru kiya jayega

 com / ez2qatoicn International Yoga Day is celebrated on 21 June worldwide
 bhartiya samskruti kii 5000 saal kii parampara main yogasana kaa kaaphi mahatv bataae gaye hai
 If you too are included in the list of people who often make excuses for not having time behind doing yoga, then start looking for another excuse for yourself now
 ji haa ab aap 5 minute main bhi khud ko feet rakh sakate hai
 Let us know 5 such postures that you can do anywhere anytime, easily by sitting on the chair
 twisting yoga-is yoga ko karne ke liye thodaa sa ghumkar apane sidhe haath ko ulte pair par rakhen or qamar main thodaa sa twist mahasoos karen
 While doing this, release the breath while filling it continuously
 yahi prakiya duusari taraf se bhi karen
 Relax the body after repeating this procedure on both sides
 uttanasana-log aksar apane pet or qamar ke paas jamaa charbi se pareshaan rahete hai
 Uttanasana is the best yogasana for such people
 is asana ko karne se aapke kandhe or haathon kii mansapeshiyaan majboot hoti hai
 To do this asana, sit upright on the chair
 baithne ke baad sabase pehle saanson ko andar khinchate hue neeche kii taraf jhuken or hatheliyon ko jameen par tikaa den
 While doing this your feet should not bend
 5 second tak isi sthiti main bane rahane ke baad saanson ko chhodte hue pehle vaali mudra main aa jaaen
 Repeat this process 10 times
 unguliyon or kalai ke liye yoga-is yoga main kursi par baithe-baithe apni kalaayiyon ko clock viz or anti-clock viz ghumaayenurdhv hastasana-is yogasana ko karne ke liye sabase pehle kursi par bilkul sidhaa baith jaaen
 Now while holding the breath in, keep both your hands up for 5 seconds
 iske baad saans chhodte hue haathon ko neeche laaen
 Repeat the same process 10 times
 aisa karte samay apni peeth or baaki sharir ko sidhaa rakhen
 By doing this Yogasana, the body gets flexibility and freshness
 kandhon ke liye yoga-is yoga main kisi kursi par sidhaa baith jaaen
 After this, rotate the shoulders with the shoulders and anti-clockwise

 is tarah se jyotiraditya sindhiya ke jimme priyanka gandhi se zyada siten ai hai

 'lajja' ke paatr mujhase real life main kolkata main mil gaye to 'besaram' kii bhoomika bani
 It is rare that a writer meets his characters
 'besaram' main nari adhikaar, maanavadhikaar, hindu-muslim ekta ke bare main likhaa
 It is up to my readers what they take from it
 julekha ke madhyam se narimukti bhi he, to suranjan kaa hindutv bhi
 My purpose is to tell that good and evil are in everyone
 hindu-musalmaan, stri-purush koi ek hi isse judaa ho aisa nahin he
 Everything happens in everyone
 6
 If we ask you, what is the caliber of your deportation? So what would you say? Who likes exile? pehle mujhe lagata tha ki main shaayad ekadin laut sakati hum
 But this hope is over
 mere bachapan ke saathi, mere sampadak, mere rishtedaar, mere apane
 
 
 Even in their pleasantries, there is a malaise to not meet them
 par maine is daur main bhi itane kaam kiye, bina kisi raajnneetik dal va sanstha se judakar jo kuch kiya, usase mujhe apane ateet par koi pachhtaawaa nahin he
 It is a matter of thinking that the secular country in which i was born in 1971 became so radical that i could not go there on the death of my mother, my Baba and my grandfather
 
 
 ( lambii saans ke saath ek chuppi) phir bhi mujhe pashchaatap nahin he, kyonki main mahilaon kii aazaadee, maanavtaa ke paksh main ladi
 i am satisfied that i am with the truth
 jiske chalate mere khilaaf fatwa bhi jari hua
 There was also an attempt to murder me
 
 
 baavjood iske main yah nahin kah sakati ki mujhe akelepan kaa ahsaas nahin hota! main bhi insaan hum, dikkat mujhe bhi mahasoos hoti he
 7
 bangladesh, europe ke kai desh, phir bharat
 
 
 West Bengal and Delhi here too? What kind of soil, people and culture did you like? There are many good people and bad people everywhere
 har desh main hai
 i have always wanted to go to my country
 main apane prakashkon, doston se milanaa chaahati hum
 Since i cannot go there, so i came to West Bengal
 bhashaa, boli or rahan sahan ke chalate yah mere liye mere duusare ghar jaisaa tha
 Here i came from Europe
 vahaan ke saare maukon ko chhod kar
 i loved Bengali, Bengali culture
 par yahaan bhi 2007 main meri kitaab bain kar di gai
 i had a second exile from here
 mere liye yah bahut dukhad sthiti he
 8
 'lajja' se 'besaram' tak, bangladesh or bharat main, bhartiya samaaj or siyasat main kya kuch badla?badlaav se bhala kise inkaar ho saktaa he, par afsos yah he ki is badlaav va vikaas main 'stri' kii sthiti main us str par badlaav nahin hua, jitna hona chahie
 The more the woman progressed, the more she was also exploited
 bangladesh main pitrusattatmak samaaj main abhi vah badlaav nahin aayaa
 Despite all the pace of development, efforts are constantly being made to suppress women
 phir hamaari saamaajik vyavastha main kai dikkatein hai
 In our matrimonial system, men maintain their relationships
 santanotpatti tak main uski apni marji nahin chalati
 If today she is allowed to get a job, then it also involves thinking of the family, husband's financial help
 mahilaayein abhi bhi paramparaagat bhoomika hi nibhaati hai
 She cannot give money to her family
 agar aap mahilaon ko sahi myanon main barabari kaa darja dena chaahate hai to aapako 'pitrusattatmak' samaaj khatm karnaa hoga
 a woman is a victim of rape only because it is filled in the boys' mind that the 'girl' is an object of your use
 aap mujhe bataaie, jo purush veshyavriti karke aata he, vah kisi bhi mahila ko acchhee najar se kaise dekh saktaa he? uske liye har stri ek 'sex object' hi rahati he! stri ko apane sharir par hi adhikaar nahin
 Even in an institution like marriage, she is a victim of rape - marital rape
 isiilie main har ladki ko yah kahati hum, apane adhikaar ke liye, sammaan ke liye vah buree bane
 As bad as she is, she will oppose the system, she will find herself
 apane sammaan va barabari ko paaegi
 9
 aap indinon kis project par kaam kar rahi hai?kuch akhabaaron main stambh likh rahi hum
 Writing poetry is reduced
 ek upanyaas or aatmakatha ke aathven bhaag par kaam kar rahi hum
 10
 abhi srilanka main carch par hamale hue
 Fanaticism is increasing all over the world
 bataur lekhak aap iskaa kya samaadhaan dekhati hai?shiksha kattarta ko khatm karne kaa eklauta madhyam he
 As long as the emphasis is on religion, this situation will not change
 rajya kaa dakhal dharm se khatm ho
 The state should not promote it in any way
 dharm hameshaa vyakti kii nijee aasthaa kaa vishay rahe
 Scientific thinking should be promoted
 vishesh baat yah ki yah kaam sabhi ko milakar karnaa hoga
 Be it Hindu, Muslim, Sikh or Christian
 sabhi ko yah samajhnaa hoga ki 'aatankwaad' dharm se hi, dharmik kattarta se hi aa rahaa he
 Hate trade has to be banned
 durbhaagya yah ki dharm logon ko sahishnu nahin kar rahaa
 It is also to be noted here that these circumstances will not change with academic education alone
 barabari, ekta, karunaa, samvednaa kii shiksha sabko di jaae
 i mean 'good education'
 inasaaniyat or maanviyata kii shiksha se he
 11
 apane prashansakon, pathakon ke liye koi sandesh?meraa apana kuch bhi nahin he
 My readers are my inspiration
 UP Election resultconstituencywise Trendsuwwara pradesh vidhansabha chunaav ke nattejey ghoshit ho gaye hai
 BJP has got a thumping majority in these elections while the ruling Samajwadi Party's alliance with Congress and Bahujan Samaj Party have been defeated badly
 bijepi ko 325, sapa-congress ko 54 to bispi ko mahaj 19 siten mili hai

 log in dilli sarkaar ne jaanaleva pradooshan se nipatane ke liye dilli main agle saal se hi BS-6 petrol or dijal laane kaa faisla kiya he
 As soon as the news comes, the question is in everyone's mind that to what extent pollution will stop only by changing petrol and diesel
 yah sawaal uthanaa isliye vaazib he kyonki sarkaar dilli main agle saal se bharat stage 6 kaa petrol or dijal to laa rahi he lekin bies-6 gaadiyaan laane kii samay seemaa philhal nahin badali gai he jo ki 2020 he
 Earlier, the time limit for bringing both Bharat Stage 6 vehicles and petrol and diesel was only 2020
 lekin dilli ke jaanaleva pradooshan par jab haahaakaar machaa tab sarkaar ne aanan-fanan main yah faisla kar liya ki dilli main april 2018 se or puure ensiaar main 2019 se bies-6 petrol or dijal hi bechaa jayega
 Petroleum expert Narendra Taneja says that this decision of the government will go a long way in reducing Delhi's pollution and people will feel relieved
 unka kahana he ki bies-4 ke mukaable bies-6 dijal main pradooshan failaane vaale khatarnaak padaarth 70 se 75 fisadi tak kam hote hai
 Narendra Taneja says that due to the absence of vehicles BS-6, it will not get immediate benefits, but in spite of this, there will be a reduction in pollution
 iske aane par khaastaur se dijal kii gadiyon se hone vaale pradooshan main badi raahat milegi kyonki nitrogen dioxide, carbon monooxide sulfur dioxide or particulet matter ke maamle main BS-6 level kaa dijal kaaphi behatar hoga
 These are dangerous polluting substances, which cause various types of diseases ranging from cancer, asthma to lungs
 khaas baat yah he ki bharat ke tamaam privet or kuch sarkari tel companiyaan pehle se hi BS-6 petrol or dijal kaa utpaadan kar to rahi hai lekin desh main koi niyam nahin hone kii vajah se yah duusare viksit deshon ko niryaat kiya ja rahaa tha lekin bharat main nahin bechaa ja rahaa tha
 But to supply BS-6 petrol diesel across Delhi and NCR on a large scale, either the government will have to ask government oil companies to improve their technology immediately or buy oil from private oil companies
 narendra taneja kaa kahana he ki bies-6 petrol or dijal kaa utpaadan mahangaa he or puure desh main ise lagu karne ke liye tel companiyon ko 50 hajaar se lekar 70 hajaar karod rupye kaa kharch karke apni rifinary ko aadhunik bananaa hoga
 One challenge will be that BS-6 petrol-diesel will be available only in Delhi from next year but in NCR this decision will be applicable from 2019
 iskaa matlab yah hua ki noida, gurugram, sonipat, faridabad, gajiabad or greater noida jaisi jagahon se bies-4 petrol or dijal lekar gaadiyaan bedadak dilli main aati jaati rahengi aurapradooshan failaati rahengi

 aise main computer banane vaali companiyaan apane notebook yaa laptop ko kuch is tarah badal rahi hai ki unke utpaadon main bhi kanjumar kii dilchaspee bani rahe
 People continue to like laptops, so their appearance and performance are being changed considerably
 desh-duniya ke bazaaron main ab dhadadhad aakarshak, patale or superfast ultrabux utaare ja rahe hai
 Actually, Ultrabook is not a technology, it is a trademark of Intel which has set its own rules for this new type of laptop
 intel kaa kahana he ki ultrabuk behad patali, bahut kam samay main shuru hone, zyada bydaree life or security se las honi chahie
 The biggest thing is that these devices should be priced around $ 1,000
 chunki ultrabuk trademark he isliye inamen bahut kam bijli khaane vaale intel ke nae siuelvi procesar or second janareshan intel aai-kor procesar hone chahie
 They should have integrated graphics, solid-state drives, unibody design as well as long-lasting batteries
 intel ke mutabik netbuk kii tulana main ultrabuk kii screen zyada badi (kam se kam 13 inch) or inaki processing power or storage kshamta bhi behatar honi chahie
 But like netbooks, ultrabooks will not have any optical or slot drives as well as many regular ports
 netbuks kii tarah ultrabux sasti to nahin, lekin suvidhaon or speed ke maamle main behatar jarur honi chahie
 Sandeep Arora, director, marketing, South Asia, Intel, says, "these smart and attractive, extremely thin devices will perform faster than ever, will have security features and will have tremendous ability to respond to user needs
" ' bahut patali, halki or khubasurat hone kii vajah se inhen lifestil accesries ke rup main khushi-khushi sweekaar kiya jayega
 Due to the long battery life and not very expensive, Intel expects Ultrabook devices to cause a lot of upheaval in the field of mobile computing
 arora ko ummid he ki intel centrino technology ne aath saal pehle mobile computing technology kaa jo kayapalat kiya tha, vaisaa hi badlaav ultrabuk bhi kar sakati he
 But it is too early to dismiss the netbook
 khaas taur par aise vakt jabaki ultrabuk kii keemat aaj bhi netbuk kii tulana main doguni se zyada he
 But many companies have announced to focus on Ultrabooks in the coming times
 ultrabux bhale hi netbuks ko khatm na karen lekin yah kaam tablet computer jarur kar rahe hai
 Ultrabooks can be an alternative to medium and expensive laptops and they too will compete with the tablet in one way or the other
 duusari peedi kii in aakarshak divices main aapke ishaaron or haav-bhav se cmand lene kii kshamta hogi or tachascreen jaisi khubiyaan bhi dikhaai dengi
 Citing a research on touch-related applications in the Ultrabook, Intel says that in a two-part design like a laptop, users have no difficulty in using the keyboard with touch on the screen
 yani ve behad aasaani se do hisson main banty ultrabuk tach kaa istemaal kar paaenge
 Says Arora, "in the future, after the use of Touch, there will be more and more new uses in the design and size of Ultrabooks
 do hisson vaali laptop kii dizin ke saath hi hybrid or canvertible saamne aaenge
 Also, there will definitely be designs that have not been conceived yet

 He was also well supported by fellow fast bowlers James Pattinson (3 for 69) and Mitchell Starc (2 for 54)
 england kaa koi bhi ballebaaj tikkar nahin khel paaya
 Jonathan Trott scored the most 48 runs for him
 toss jitkar pehle ballebaaji ke liye utre england kaa score chaay ke vishram ke samay chah wicket par 185 ran tha lekin iske baad patinson or stark ne do-do wicket baantkar uske nichle kram ko jaldi sametane main der nahin lagaai
 These included the wicket of Jani Bairsta, who played a struggling 37-run innings
 australia kaa palada haalanki sidle ne baari rakhaa
 The batsmen who showed the way to the pavilion include Kevin Pietersen (14) and Trott
 pichhali baar ashes ke shuruaati din hetric banane vaale sidle ne jo root (30) ke rup main pehla wicket liya
 He broke his 54-run partnership for the fifth wicket with Bairsta by getting Ian Bell (25) caught by Shane Watson in the first slip
 wicketiper ballebaaj mat praayar (1) ne sidle kii baahar jaati gend par karaara shaat jamaaya lekin vah sidhe cover point par khadey philip huge ke haathon main chalaa gaya
 In this way, Siddle was successful in taking five or more wickets in the innings for the eighth time in his career
 isse pehle cook ne toss jitkar pehle ballebaaji kaa faisla kiya lekin aasmaan par badal hone ke kaaran swing gendbaajon ko acchhee madad mili
 Cook had scored 766 runs in Australia's 31 win over the Ashes in 201011 in Australia
 lekin ashes test main pehali baar captaini kar rahaa baayen haath kaa yah ballebaaj keval 13 ran banaakar out ho gaya
 Pattinson bowled well from the start and troubled both Cook and Root outside the off stump
 cook ne isi tarah kii gend ko apane kadamon kaa istemaal kiye bina push karne kii koshish kii jo unke balle kaa kinaaraa lekar wicketiper bed hadine ke dastaanon main chali gai
 Trott soon regained rhythm
 unhone patinson par cover drive se chaukaa jamaaya or apana pehla test match khel rahe baayen haath ke spinner 19 varshiya eston edgar kaa swaagat bhi chauke se kiya
 Siddle broke his 51-run partnership with Trott by taking the wicket of Joe Root (30) on the first ball after changing ends
 tippaniyan Pietersen had scored just one run when his glans dived off Pattinson's ball , but could not contain Haddin's glove
 lunch ke samay england kaa score do wicket par 98 ran tha lekin usne duusare satr ke shuru main hi petersan kaa wicket ganvaa diya jinhone sidle kii baahar jaati gend par beparwaah shaat khelkar australian captain maaikel clark ko kaich thamaya
 Trott looked good on touch and hit nine boundaries in his innings
 unhone bhi baahar jaati gend apane viketon par maari
 Bell again failed to score in the odd conditions and gave an easy catch to Watson off Siddle
 nichle kram ke ballebaajon main keval stuart broad (24) hi kuch yogadan de paae

 inamen jaani beresta kaa wicket bhi shaamil tha jinhone 37 ran kii sangharmpurn pari kheli

 unhone jin ballebaajon ko pavilion kii raah dikhaai unamem kevin petersan (14) or traat bhi shaamil hai
 Siddle, who scored a hat-trick on the opening day of the Ashes, took the first wicket as Joe Root (30)
 unhone ian bel (25) ko pehali slip main shen watasan ke haathon kaich karakar beresta ke saath unki paanchaven wicket ke liye 54 ran kii saajhedaari todi

 is tarah se sidle apane kariyar main aathvin baar pari main paanch yaa isse adhik wicket lene main safal rahe

 cook ne australia main 2010-11 main england kii ashes main 3-1 se jeet ke dauraan 766 ran banaae the
 But this left-handed batsman, captaining for the first time in the Ashes Test, was dismissed for only 13 runs
 patinson ne shuru se acchhee gendbaaji kii tathaa cook or root donon ko aaf stump ke baahar pareshaan kiya
 Cook tried to push a similar ball without using his footsteps which took the edge of his bat and went into the gloves of wicketkeeper Bad Haddin
 traat jald hi lay main aa gaye
 He struck Pattinson with a cover drive and also welcomed 19-year-old Aston Agar, a left-arm spinner, playing his first Test match with a four
 sidle ne chor badalane ke baad pehali gend par hi jo root (30) ke wicket ukhadkar trot ke saath unki 51 ran kii saajhedaari todi
 The comments petersan ne tab keval ek ran banaaya tha jab patinson kii gend par unka glance dive lagane ke baavjood bhi hadine ke dastaane main nahin samaa paaya
 England's score at lunch was 98 for two, but they lost the wicket of Pietersen early in the second season, who caught a carefree shot off Siddle's outing ball to Australian captain Michael Clarke
 trot acchhee tach main dikh rahe the or unhone apni pari main nau chauke lagaae
 He also hit the ball going out on his wickets
 bel phir se visham paristhitiyon main ran banane main naakaam rahe or sidle kii gend par watasan ko aasaan kaich de baithe
 Among lower-order batsmen, only Stuart Broad (24) was able to contribute

 mumbai ke breabourne stadium main ravivaar ko hone vaale mahila vishwa cap ke final main paanch baar kii champion australia kaa saamana westeindies se hoga
 This is the tenth edition of the Women's World Cup, started in 1973 and India is hosting it for the third time
 toornament ke final main pahunchi donon tiimon ne hi visham paristhitiyon main shandaar pradarshan karte hue final kaa rasta tay kiya he
 While Australia, by far the most successful team in the history of the tournament, has won all the matches in the tournament except for the loss in their last Super League match, the West Indies beat Australia to secure their place in the final
 isse pehle, carabian mahila khilaadiyon ne super-6 maichon ke sabhi teen pramukh mukaable jeetne se pehle super-6 main apni jagah banane ke liye keval group str par ek hi muqabla jeeta tha
 The West Indies had won the last league match against Australia, showing the previous champions England and New Zealand out of the tournament
 australia ke final tak ke safar ke dauraan sabhi khilaadiyon ne behtareen pradarshan kaa mujahiraa kiya
 Australian paceman Magan has performed particularly well
 unhone or anyaa shrubsol ne toornament main sabase zyada 13 wicket jatke hai
 Australia's legendary spinner Lisa Sthalekar and her partner Irene Osborne have bowled tight and tight in the middle overs of the innings
 lekin vahiin australia kii ballebaaji puure toornament ke dauraan apeksha ke anukool nahin rahi
 Rachel Haynes has scored the most 221 runs in six matches with two half-centuries, excluding the rest
 vahiin, pehali baar vishwa cap final main jagah banane vaali vestiindis kii team par group str muqablon main england se haarane ke baad toornament se baahar hone kaa khatra mandara gaya tha
 But the West Indies made it to the finals, performing brilliantly in subsequent matches
 vestiindis kii captain marisa angulira ne kaha ki yah toornament unke liye kaaphi utaar-chadhaav bharaa rahaa
